returns a `PdfGestureDetails` object, which contains both sets of coordinates[1]:\n\n*   **`details.pagePosition`**:

`Offset` of the tapped location on the **PDF Viewer widget** (screen coordinates)[1].\n*   **`details.pageNumber`**:

to render visually as portrait. \\n   Our visual overlay calculations (`_getWPageZoomed()` and `_getHPageZoomed()`) do 
not check the rotation metadata of the page when calculating visual dimensions on the screen. As a result, width and 
height are swapped in our code, and the maximum page height is incorrectly calculated (e.g., `600` instead of `800` 
pixels). Clamping the relative coordinates to `[0.0, 1.0]` blocks dragging the signature below the calculated bottom 
boundary (`600` pixels), making it impossible to drag the signature into the bottom quarter of the page.\\n2. 
**Incorrect Baking Location:** Since the visual coordinates are computed based on incorrect page boundaries (due to 
the page dimensions swap) and out-of-sync scroll tracking from `ScrollNotification` (which includes nested component 
notifications or layout offsets), the computed relative placement coordinates `_overlayRx` and `_overlayRy` are 
incorrect. During the `Bake` process, these incorrect relative coordinates are applied to the physical page, resulting 
in incorrect placement.\\n\\n## Proposed Changes\\n\\n### [Component Name] Flutter Editor Layout and 
Calculations\\n\\n#### [MODIFY] [main.dart](file:///c:/coding/antigravity%20coding/signature-addon/lib/main.dart)\\n- 
**Track Page Rotations:** Add a state variable `List<int> _pdfPageRotations = []` and populate it inside 
`onDocumentLoaded` by reading `page.rotation` (e.g., 0, 90, 180, 270) for each page.\\n- **Rotation-Aware Dimension 
Calculations:** Update `_getWPageZoomed()`, `_getHPageZoomed()`, and `_getPage\n<truncated 1334
